April 30th, 09:05am, 2019, training without mixup, with 256 filters in the first layer, and delete the 3*3 in the bottom of V.

summary:
1  This network used 256 filters in the 1st layer,and deleted the feature map of size 3*3 in the bottom of V model; It got a test dice of 63%. It looks its result is worse than than 128 filters at 1st layer with 3*3 feature map at bottom of V model (71% test dice);
2  It shows that the deeper layer, instead more filters, will helpful;
3  Last weekend the mixup crossing-class augmentation experiment got a test dice of 60% with a same model above. Maybe it needs to debug the alpha parameter of B distribution of mixup.
4  Today I am going to add an extra 3*3 convolutional layer inside each layer of V model, because the above experiment shows deeper layers will be helpful.

May 1st, 09:00, 2019

After adding 4 conv layers in each layer of V Model, the test dice can get 73% with TPR 92%

Summary:
1  Yesterday, I added 4 convolutional layers with a residual edge in each layer of V model,which is like the integrated effect of overlap of 4 single V models. The rationality behind this is that cancer segmentation is more complicated than organ segmenation, there are no two cancer with same shape.Therefore we need to more complicated network to capture the boundaries.
2  After one night training, it can reach test dice of 73.3% with TPR 92%;  
3  Currently network used Crossing Entropy and Boundary Loss with reward, and image Jitters with radius 5 which make image extremely fuzzy (maybe be 5 is too big image jitter for this segmenation);
4  Today, I will adjust the Loss function and Jitters parameter, I believe it will further improve accuracy;
